Umnqopho wewebhusayidi yemiSebenzi yomBuso weSewula Afrika kunikela ngomthombo munye welwazi ngemisebenzi enikelwa mbuso weSewula Afrika . .
Umnqopho kukwehlisa ukungalingani okukhona phakathi kwalabo abanikelwe amandla nalabo abangakanikelwa , umnotho wokuthoma newesibili . .
Iwebhusayidi kungenelela okuqakathekileko okuhlose ukuqinisekisa bonyana izakhamuzi zizakukghona ukuthintana nombuso . .
Abasebenzisi abahlosiweko balewebhusayithi zizakhamuzi zeSewula Afrika kiwo woke amahlangothi wenarha , amabhizinisi weSewula Afrika akhona nasazokuba khona namkha iinhlangano , izakhamizi neenhlangano ezibuya kwezinye iinarha ezifuna imisebenzi embusweni weSewula afrika . .
Ikoro eqakathekileko yabasebenzisi ibunjwa ziinkhungo zokungenelela ezifana nama Community Centres ( ama ) , abaSebenzi bokuThuthukiswa komPhakathi ( ama ) kanye ne Pele Gateway Call Centre , ezizakurhelebha ukukghonakalisa ukusetjenziswa kwewebhusayidi ngilabo abangakghoniko ukusebenzisa bunqopha i . .
Ubungako belwazi elikulewebhusayidi .
Ilwazi ngemisebenzi yombuso .
Iwebhusayidi inelwazi ngemisebenzi yombuso enikelwa ezingeni lombuso wesitjhaba . .
Ilwazi ngemisebenzi lihlukaniswa ngokuya kwemihlobo emithathu yemisebenzi : .
Imisebenzi eyenzelwa abantu : imisebenzi eyenzelwa izakhamuzi zeSewula Afrika ehlelwe ngokuya kwezehlakalo zepilo .
Imisebenzi eyenzelwa iinhlangano : imisebenzi ekhambelana neenhlangano namabhizinisi .
Imisebenzi eyenzelwa amaphandle : ilwazi eliqaliswe ezakhamizini zeenarha zangaphandle ezifuna imisebenzi efaneleko embusweni weSewula Afrika . .
Elinye nelinye lamahlangothi la libunjwa ngendlela ekhambisana nokulandelana kwezehlakalo zepilo ( izehlakalo ezitholakala epilweni yesakhamuzi namkha ibhizinisi ) . .
Izehlakalo zepilo godu zihlukaniswa ngokuya kweengaba zepilo . .
Ilwazi ngomunye nomunye umsebenzi lihlelwa ngokuya kweendawo ezilikhomba eziqakathekileko , oku , yihlathululo : amagadango okufanele alandelwe ; imithetho esetjenziswako ; amazinga wokusebenza nesikhathi ; iindleko ; amaforomo azaliswako nemininingwana yokuthintana . .
Ilwazi elikhambelanako .
Isigabesi sewebhusayidi sivezwa ngebha yokuzuma ilwazi ku , inamathintwano akhambelana namawebhusayidi walesosehlakalo sepilo . .
Amalimi .
Kilewebhusayidi kutholakala amalimi ali , okungilawa i , Afrikaans , isiNdebele , isiXhosa , isiZulu , isiPedi , isiSuthu , isiTsonga , isiVenda , iSiswati kunye nesiTswana . .
Ilwazi lokusebenzela litlolwe ngesiNgisi , kuthi ngemva kwalokho litjhugululelwe kwamanye amalimi . .
Ilwazi lokusebenzela ngamanye amalimi libekwa webhusayidi ngemva kokutjhugululwa . .
Ezinye iimbumbi zewebhusayidi .
Sebenzisa ikhasi lokuthintana nathi ( Thintana nathi ) ukuveza imibono namkha ukubuza ngewebhusayidi yemiSebenzi yomBuso . .
Ithintwano www.gov.za linikela ngokufikelela ikhasi le lomBuso weSewula Afrika , elinikela ngokufikelela lewebhusayidi ( iwebhusayidi yemiSebenzi yomBuso ) kanye newebhusayidi yeLwazi ngomBuso ( www.info.gov.za ) . .
Umebhe wesayithi unikela ngesithombe esibonwako sesakhiwo sewebhusayidi . .
Senziwe ngokweenkhundla , sephula ilwazi lesayithi libe ziindawo zeenhloko ezithileko . .
Ngalokho likukghonakalisa ukuzijayeza mayelana nokungaphakathi kwesakhiwo sewebhusayidi . .
Ikhasi lekhaya linikela ngerhemo lemisebenzi efikelelwa khulu . .
Okufakiweko kunikela ngokufikelela emisebenzini okungemikhulu emihlanu evakatjhelwa basebenzisi . .
Irhemo litjhugululwa ngokuya kweembalobalo zamakhasi avakatjhelweko . .
Ibhoksi lokuzuma likhona kiwo woke amakhasi wewebhusayidi . .
Lokha nawufaka i yokuzuma , iwebhusayidi ezeleko izakuzunywa bona kutholakale amagama lawo . .
Godu ungenza ukuzuma okungcono khulu ngokukhetha ithintwano lokuZuma okuNgcono Khulu . .
Ukuzuma lokhu kuzuma ilwazi kwamanye amawebhusayidi wombuso . .
Amathintwano namawebhusayidi wangaphandle atjengiswa ngamagama athi ' Outside link ' ( ithintwano langaphandle ) elivela ebhoksini lokha ikhesa nayikhamba phezu kwethintwano . .
Iwebhusayidi izakuvula iwindo lebhrawuza elitja . .
Izinga lokulethwa ebujameni banjesi .
Iwebhusayidi ilethwa ebujameni banjesi njalo njalo . .
Umthethomgomo wethu kunikela ngelwazi lokha nalithoma ukutholakala . .
Kodwana , abathuthukisi bewebhusayidi yemiSebenzi yomBuso angeze baqinisekisa bona ilwazi elivezwa emawebhusayidini esithintana nawo ngelanjesi . .
Qala iimFuno noBujamo , indima 4.3 . .
Ubunikazi belwazi .
Iminyango yombuso banikazi belwazi elisemawebhusayidini wayo . .
Lomsebenzi unikelwa abaphathi bokuthintana beminyango , abasebenza ukuphatha ilwazi elivezwa ewebhusayidini . .
I Communications ( GCIS ) isebenza ukuphathwa mazombe nokukhanjelaniswa kokungaphakathi kwewebhusayidi . .
Ubunjalo bomtlolo .
Indlela yokuvezwa kwelwazi webhusayidi yi . .
Kodwana , imihlobo ye yemitlolo ( isibonelo , imiThetho , amaforomo ) inikelwa ukugcina ubunjalo bokuthoma bomtlolo . .
Ukuvula imitlolo ye , utlhoga ukuba ne- Adobe Acrobat Reader 4 namkha engaphezulu kwale bona ifakwe ekhomphyutheni yakho . .
Izakuvula imitlolo bunqopha ebhrawuzeni yakho . .
Kwesinye isikhathi kuthatha isikhathi ukuvula imitlolo ye . .
Kilokhu , siphakamisa bona uyikhuphele ekhomphyutheni yakho bewuyivule ukusuka lapho . .
Isiyeleliso zokukhupha imitlolo uyise ekhomphyutheni yakho : .
Lokha nawusebenzisa i Explorer njengebhrawuza yakho .
Ngemawusi yakho , gandelela ngesidleni umtlolo ofuna ukukhupha . .
Ku menu , khetha ' Save target as ( Bulunga ithagethi njenge ) ' . .
Ewindweni elithi ' Bulunga Njenge ' , khetha indawo ku drive lapho ufuna ukubulungela umtlolo bewugandelele ibhathini ethi ' Bulunga ' . .
Ifayili izakukhutjhwa isiwe endaweni oyikhethileko . .
Vula i Reader yakho bewuvule imitlolo oyikhuphileko . .
Lokha nawusebenzisa i njengebhrawuza yakho .
Gandelelela phasi ibhathini ethi , kuthi ngemawusi yakho ugandelele ngesinceleni sayo ethintanweni lomtlolo ofuna ukuwubulunga . .
Ewindweni elithi ' Bulunga ' khetha indawo ku drive lapho ufuna ukubulunga umtlolo bewugandelele ibhathini ethi ' Bulunga ' . .
Ifayili izakukhutjhwa isiwe endaweni oyikhethileko . .
Vula isiFundo Acrobat sakho bewuvule imitlolo oyikhuphileko . .
Ufuna irhelebho ngemiraro oyifumene kilewebhusayidi ? .
Sibawa usithinte ( electronic@gcis.gov.za ) nayikuthi uhlangabezana nemiraro kilewebhusayidi . .
Nangabe ihlangano yebumbano , ikhampani , namkha ikhampani yehlanganyela ayisakwazi ukubhadala iinkolodo namkha ifezakalise iimbopho zayo ( ngenca yokutjhona , ukungalawuleki kuhle namkha kungaba ngimuphi unobangela ) , umNqophisi wezeRhwebo namaBubulo kungenzeka ayilawule namkha ayivale leyo bhizimisi . .
Ihlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana , namkha elinye nelinye ilunga lehlangano namkha nanyana ngubani onekareko angenza isibawo ekhotho kobana ihlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana ilawulwe ngumNqophisi namkha ivalwe . .
Ikhotho ezokulalela isibawo leso makube liphiko lekhotho ekulu namkha iKhotho kaMarhastrada enamandla wokulawula ubulungiswa endaweni lapho ihlangano yebumbano leyo isebenzela khona . .
Ikhotho ingathatha leso siqunto nakube kuyindlela elungileko . .
Nangabe ikhotho ibeka umNqophisi bonyana alawule ihlangano yebumbano leyo namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana leyo , uzakuba negunya lokuphatha iindaba zehlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana ngokuya ngemibandela yemiThetho yemaKhampani , 1973 . .
Nangabe ihlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana yenza isibawo ngokutlolela umNqophisi , angayesula ihlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana nangabe uyaneliseka nge : .
Isiqunto sokobanyana isulwe sathathwa emhlanganweni ogade ukhanjelwe linani elikhulu lamalunga wehlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana ; .
Isiqunto samukelwe linengi lamalunga agade akhona emhlanganweni , begodu .
Zoke iindaba ebekumele zikhulunywe ngaphambi kokwesulwa , kufaka hlangana indlela ipahla kunye neenkwelede zehlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana zizakusetjenzwa ngayo . .
Nangabe ikhotho ithatha isiqunto sokuvala ihlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yebumbano yesikhatjhana , izakuqunta bonyana ipahla yehlangano leyo izakuhlukaniswa ngokulinganako nangokuthembeka . .
Ikhotho izakuyelela zoke iimphakamiso ezizakwenziwa mNqophisi manqophana nokwabiwa kwepahla . .
Nangabe umNqophisi namkha ihlangano yebumbano namkha ihlangano yesikhatjhana , elinye nelinye ilunga lehlangano namkha omunye nomunye umuntu onekareko wenza isibawo sokobanyana ihlangano leyo ilawulwe mNqophisi namkha ivalwe , uNgqongqotjhe uzakunikela ikambiso okumele ihlangano leyo ilawulwe ngayo ngumNqophisi namkha ivalwe . .
UNgqongqotjhe uzakunikela umNqophisi amandla kunye nomsebenzi , isiPhathiswa sokuTlolisa , ihlangano , amalunga kunye neenhlanganao ezinekareko kilesi simo . .
Endabeni yekhampani namkha ikhampani yehlanganyela I , enye nenye ihlangano enekareko , umnqophisi namkha umhloli weencwadi zekhampani , I- South African Revenue Service ( SARS ) namkha umTlolisi wamaKhampani angenza isibawo sokwesula kwekhampani namkha I . .
Ukuphathwa ngokuhlukileko ngakwezomthelo kunikelwa iinhlangano ezingenzi inzuzo ezihlonyelwe bona kuzuze umphakathi . .
Kodwana lokhu kuphathwa ngokuhlukileko ngakwezomthelo kunikelwa kuphela iinhlangano ezikhambisana neenjamiso zomThetho weenHlangano eziNgenzi iNzuzo ka nemithetho ekhambelanako . .
Iinhlangano ezifisa ukwenza isibawo sokubekelwa ngeqadi ekubhadeleni umthelo kufanele ziwele ngakwelinye lamahlangothi alandelako : .
Ikhampani ewela ngaphasi kwesiGaba 21 somThetho wamaKhampani ka . .
Ikhampani yesiGaba 21 enememorandamu nama of association kanye nestatimende sokusungula begodu netloliswe noMtlolisi wamaKhampani . .
I enomtlolo wokusungula kanye ne deed , etloliswe no of the High Court . .
Ihlanganisela yabantu . .
Ihlangano yokuzithandela yabantu iphethwe mthethosisekelo . .
Lapho isitatimende sokusungula nasingakhambisaniko neenjamiso zesiGaba 30 somThetho weenHlangano eziNgenzi iNzuzo ka isibawo kufanele siphekelelwe sibopho esitloliweko esitlikitlwe mbawi . .
Ukubekelwa ngaphandle okudlulileko kuzakuragela phambili nokusebenza bekube sikhathi lapho umbawi aziswe yi African Revenue Service ( SARS ) ngokuthathwa kwesiqunto ngokuya komthetho omutjha . .
Iinhlangano kwanjesi ezingabekelwa ngeqadi ngokuya komthetho ekubhadeleni umthelo wengeniso zingaletha iforomo elizalisiweko lesibawo nemitlolo esekelako kanye nesibopho esitlikitliweko lapho abantu abasebenzisa isikhundla se bathembisa ukukhambisana neenjamiso zesiGaba 30 somThetho weenHlangano eziNgenzi iNzuzo ka . .
Imitlolo yokusekela elandelako kufanele iphekelele isibawo : .
ikhampani : Namathisela ikhophi yeMemorandamu nama of Association ( kufaka amakhophi weenqunto zoke ezitlolisiweko ezitjhugulula imemorandamu nama ) .
i : Namathisela ikhophi ye deed kanye netjhuguluko elilandelako lama of amendment .
ihlanganisela yabantu : Namathisela ikhophi yomthethosisekelo wamuva nje . .
Iinhlangano ezihlonywe ngomnqopho wokunikela ngama , imifundalize nabonongorwana bezefundo , irhubhululo kanye nokufundisa , ukungezelela imitlolo yokusekela engehla , kufanele godu zizalise iNcwadi yesiBopho esiTloliweko EI 3 . .
Iinkolo zombuso nezizijameleko ( zangeqadi ) , iinkhungo zefundo ephakamileko , iinkhungo zefundo nebandulo labadala ( ama ) , kanye neenkhungo zefundo nebandulo eliragela phambili kufanele zinamathisele ikhophi yesitifikeyidi sokuzitlolisa esikhutjhwe ngabasemaGunyeni bezeFundo abafaneleko .
Isondlo sibopho sokubonelela omunye umuntu , isibonelo , umntwana , ngendlu , ukudla , izembatho , ifundo netlhogomelo lezokwelatjhwa , namkha ngokhunye okungatlhogeka ukunikela ngalezi zinto eziqakathekileko . .
Lesi sibopho somthetho sokondla sibizwa ' ngesibopho sesondlo ' namkha ' ngesibopho sokusekela ' . .
Ngubani okufanele anikele ngesondlo ? .
Isibopho sokondla sisekelwe etjhebiswaneni leengazi , loku namkha eqinisweni lokobana abantu laba batjhadile . .
Umntwana kufanele asekelwe namkha ondliwe : .
babelethi bakhe , nanyana batjhadile , bahlala bobabili , bahlala ngokuhlukana namkha bahlukanisile , kufaka ababelethi aba umntwana ; kanye / namkha .
ugogo nobamkhulu bakhe , nanyana ababelethi bomntwana bebatjhadile . .
Kodwana lokhu kuhluka ubujamo nobujamo . .
Isibopho sokusekela ilunga lomndeni asipheleli ekusekeleni umntwana . .
Elinye nelinye ilunga lomndeni , kungaqalwa ubudala , lingabawa elinye ilunga ukubasekela namkha ukubondla , kuye ngokuthi ubujamo obulandelako kuhlangabezanwa nabo : .
Ilunga lomndeni elifuna ukusekelwa alikghoni ukuzisekela . .
Ilunga lomndeni okufunwa kilo imali yesondlo alikghoni ukubhadela imali yesondlo efunekako . .
Ngiziphi iindleko ezingafunwa ? .
Ungafuna isekelo elizwakalako elitlhogekako ukuqalelela umntwana namkha umuntu onelungelo lesondlo ngezinga lokuphila elifaneleko kanye nokukhulisa . .
Lokhu kufaka ukunikela ngezinto eziqakathekileko ezifana nokudla , izembatho nendlu , kanye nokubhadela ifundo elungileko . .
Ikhotho godu ingalaya uyise womntwana ukufaka isandla ekubhadelweni kweendleko zokuphila ukuthoma ngelanga umntwana abelethwa ngalo ukufika ngelanga okukhutjhwa ngalo umlayo wesondlo . .
Ikhotho godu inganikela ngomlayo wokubhadelwa kweendleko zokwelapha namkha ilaye bona umntwana atloliswe ehlelweni lezokwelapha lomunye wabathintekako njengomthembele kibo . .
Ukukghonakalisa ikhotho ukunikela ngomlayo wesondlo olungileko , bobabili abathintekako kufanele banikele ikhotho ubufakazi beendleko . .
Umbono wakho ngokuziphatha komunye umbelethi awunamphumela elungelweni lomntwanakho lokobana ondliwe . Usezakubhadela isondlo nanyana omunye umbelethi .
atjhada butjha .
azibandakanya kwelinye itjhebiswano .
angakuvumeli ukubona abantwana .
laba nabanye abantwana ngokukhamba kwesikhathi . .
Isibopho sakho sokubhadela imali yesondlo kanye nelungelo lakho lokufikelela abantwana ziindaba ezihlukeneko begodu azikhambelani . .
Ukudlula lapho , abantwana bomunye nomunye othintekako abanamthelela esibopheni sokusekela . .
Kodwana inani lesondlo elizakubhadelwa lingatjhugululwa yikhotho nayikuthi omunye wabathintekako angaletha isibawo . .
Amagadango okufanele alandelwe .
Yenza isibawo sesondlo ekhotho kamarhastrada esiyingini lapho uhlala khona . .
Nayikuthi uyasola , ikhotho yendawo izakutjela bona usenze kuyiphi ikhotho isibawo . .
Tjhinga ekhotho efaneleko bewuzalise iForomo A : Application for a maintenance order ( Isibawo somlayo wesondlo ) . .
Ukungezelela eforomini elizalisiweko , letha ubufakazi bengeniso yakho yenyanga kanye neendleko , obufana namarasidi wokuthenga ukudla , igezi kanye / namkha ukubhadelwa kwesikolodo serente . .
Ikhotho izakubeka ilanga wena noziphendulelako ( umuntu ofuna abhadele isondlo ) enizakuya ngalo ekhotho . .
Isiphathiswa sezondlo kanye nomphenyi bazakuphenya isibawo sakho sokufuna isondlo begodu bazakutjheja ubujamo bakho . .
Ikhotho izakunikela amasamoni ( okuyincwadi ekulaya bona uvele ekhotho ) umuntu oziphendulelako ukuvela ekhotho ngelanga elithileko ukukhulumisana ngendaba . .
Umuntu oziphendulelako angavuma ukubhadela imali efunwako namkha ayiphikise ekhotho . .
Nayikuthi umuntu oziphendulelako uyavuma ukubhadela isondlo , umarhastrada uzakubuyekeza imitlolo leyo . .
Uzakwenza umlayo begodu uzakuqunta ukwenza njalo ngaphandle kokubawa abathintekako ukuvela ekhotho . .
Nayikuthi umuntu okuthiwa kufanele abhadele isondlo akavumelani nokukhutjhwa komlayo , kufanele avele ekhotho , lapho ubufakazi , abathintekako kanye nabofakazi babo bazakulalelwa khona . .
Nayikuthi ikhotho ifumana bona umuntu kufanele abhadele imali yesondlo , izakwenza umlayo wenani okufanele libhadelwe . .
Ikhotho nayo izakuqunta bona ukubhadelwa kuzakwenziwa nini begodu njani . .
Ikhotho ingalaya bona imali yesondlo ibhadelwe ngenye yeendlela ezilandelako : .
E lakamarhastrada wendawo namkha e elinye lombuso elenzelwe lomnqopho . .
E yebhanga namkha ye society ekhonjwe mumuntu othintekako . .
Bunqopha emuntwini okufanele afumane imali . .
Ngokusebenzisa umlayo obeka bona umqatjhi nguye okufanele abhadele isondlo ngokudoswa kwemali bunqopha emrholweni womsebenzi , ngokukhambisana nomThetho weSondlo ka omutjha . .
Iforomo lesibawo kufanele lizaliswe mbawi ingasi omunye umuntu , nakungasi njalo isibawo asizukutjhejwa . .
Sibawa ufunde umhlahlandlela wesibawo ukukurhelebha ekambisweni yakho yelayisense . .
Esigabeni somHlobo wetlayendi : .
qala ibhoksana loLetha ngeNarheni ngaphasi kokutlolisa . .

isabhabhu lapho ibhizinisi litholakala khona .

ngubani ozakutlama nokuletha imitlolo kwa African Revenue Service .
nokobana uzakutlama bewulethe imitlolo namkha umsebenzeli uzakuqatjhwa ukwenza njalo .
Isigaba seGunya lokwenza isiBawo kufanele sizaliswe mumuntu ( nguSomabhizinisi oyi proprietor , Mnqophisi , ma , liLunga , yi namkha mumuntu ophethe enye nenye ihlangano ) owenza isibawo sokuzitlolisa njengoletha ipahla ngenarheni . .
Igama lombawi namkha igama lokuzitlolisa lehlangano , ingasi igama lokwenza ibhizinisi kufanele livezwe kileli ziko . .
Nakuvela i ( * ) , sula lokho okufaneleko . .
esigabeni sesiFungo , veza okulandelako : .
ama nesibongo somuntu owenza isibawo selayisense .
ubujamo bomuntu owenza isibawo , isibonelo , umNqophisi , umPhathi , uMnikazi .
umuntu owenza isibawo kufanele atlikitle iforomo lesibawo .
ilanga okutlikitlwe ngalo isibawo .
indawo lapho kwatlikitlelwa isibawo . .
Zalisa iforomo lesibawo bewulilethe e eliseduze lomThelo wePahla le African Revenue Service . .
Namathisela amakhophi wamambala namkha aqinisekisiweko wokulandelako : .
imvumo yomNyango wezokuRhwebelana namaBubulo nayifunekako .
indlela yokwenza nayikuthi wenza isibawo ngaphasi kwe yokubuyiselwa imali oyibhadeleko 607.04.10(02) , 607.04.10(03) , 607.04.10(09) no 607.04.10(12) .
iincwadi zokuzazisa ebujameni besakhamuzi seSewula Afrika .
imitlolo yamaphaspoti ebujameni bomuntu ongasi sisakhamuzi : .
umuntu .
ama aku corporation aku - woke amalunga namkha ama namkha ama .
ikhampani - boke abanqophisi , kufaka umNqophisi oPhetheko noMnqophisi weeMali . .
Umbawi , ingasi omunye wesithathu kufanele azalise iforomo lesibawo ( i 185 ) , nakungasi njalo isibawo asizukutjhejwa . .
Esigabeni somHlobo wetlayendi ( A ) qalisisa ibhoksana lokuBuyiselwa umthelo , esigabeni sokuzitlolisa . .
Esigabeni semininingwana yezokuRhwebelana ( umHlobo wetlayendi II ) , kufanele uveze : .
igama lokwenza ibhizinisi lebhizinisi lakho .
igama lesitrada nenomboro yesitolo esifuna ukubuyiselwa imali yomthelo .
igama nenomboro yefluru yomakho okwenziwa kiwo ibhizinisi .
isabhabhu lapho ibhizinisi itholakala khona .

Ikhampani yangaphetjheya ayikavunyelwa ukuzitlolisa eSewula Afrika . .
Yikhampani kuphela yeSewula Afrika , isakhamuzi seSewula Afrika namkha ihlangano yangokomthetho eSewula Afrika engenza isibawo sokutloliswa kokudla kweenonisi . .
Iinonisi zesiQhema 1 ngilezo ezinenayithrojini , ifosforasi namkha iphotheziyamu njengesinongo esikhulu , godu zaziwa ngeenonisi ze . .
Ukutloliswa kunikelwa kuphela nayikuthi ngesikhathi sokutloliswa : .
isibumbeko sesinonisi esithintentako akukafaneli sihluke esibumbekweni esitlolisiweko .
imininingwana nehlelo lamagama aselebuleni namkha esimumathini , angeze atjhugululwa ngaphandle kwemvumo yangaphambi kwesikhathi ebuya emTlolisini .
ubujamo obubekwe phasi ngesikhathi sokutloliswa kukhanjiswana nabo .
ukutloliswa angeze kwadluliswa .
ubukhulu besikhwama namkha besimumathi angeze batjhugululwa ngaphandle kwemvumo yangaphambilini ebuya emTlolisini . .
Isibawo sokutloliswa kokudla kwefuyo neenonisi sibunjwa , yincwadi ephekelela isibawo ebuya emnikazini wokutloliswa namkha umjameli okhonjiweko . .
Incwadi kufanele ifake : .
igama lomkhiqizo .
inomboro yokutloliswa nayikuthi umkhiqizo sele utlolisiwe .
ibanga lokulethwa ( nanyana kusibawo esitjha , isibawo setjhuguluko , isibawo sokutloliswa komkhiqizo osukela komunye ) .
iincwadi zemvumo ezibuya emnikazini wokutloliswa ziyafuneka ( imvumo yokutloliswa komkhiqizo osuselwa komunye namkha imvumo yokusebenzisa igama lomkhiqizo namkha ilebula yenye ihlangano ) .
imali elungileko yesibawo .
amatjhege athunyelwa ngokwehlukana nesibawo kufanele aphekelelwe yincwadi ehlathululako ( amatjhege namaposoda kufanele enziwe abhadele u : Agriculture ) .
ikhasi lendlela yokwenziwa kwesinonisi . .
Letha iforomo lesibawo eembaweni ezitjha nematjhugulukweni ekutlolisweni okukhona , kufaka ukutjhugululwa kwendlela yokwenziwa . .
Letha amaforomo wesibawo ngeduplikheyithi u zalise amaforomo ngokuzeleko , ngaphandle kokukhuluma ngeembawo ezidlulileko , iinomboro zamakhasi namkha imikhiqizo ( ubuncani bakhona ikhophi yinye yamaforomo wesibawo kufanele ibe netlikitlo lamambala . .
Elinye kufanele kube yikhophi ) . .
Umuntu okhonjwe ngokomthetho , okwenyulwa bona kube mumuntu umTlolisi azakuthintana nekhampani ngaye , kufanele atlikitle amaforomo weembawo . .
Igama nenomboro yokutloliswa komkhiqizo kufanele isetjenziswe njengombana kubekwe esitifikeyidini sokutloliswa . .
Elinye itjhuguluko egameni , nanyana lilincani kangangani , lizakuthathwa njengetjhuguluko . .

Ikhampani yangaphetjheya angeze yenza isibawo sokuzitlolisa eSewula Afrika . .
Yikhampani etloliswe kuphela ekhaya , isakhamuzi seSewula Afrika namkha ihlangano yangokomthetho etloliswe eSewula Afrika engenza isibawo sokutloliswa kokudla kwefuyo neenonisi . .
Iinonisi zesiQhema 2 ngilezo ezinokuphilako okukhulu nokuncani njengesinongo esikhulu , godu zaziwa njengeenonisi ze . .
Ukutloliswa kunikelwa kuphela nayikuthi ngesikhathi sokutloliswa : .
ukubunjwa kwesinonisi esithintekako angeze kwahluka esibumbini esitlolisiweko .
imininingwana namagama elebuleni namkha esimumathini angeze yatjhugululwa ngaphandle kwemvumo etloliweko efunyenwe ngaphambilini yomTlolisi .

Incwadi ephekelela isibawo kufanele ifake : .
igama lomkhiqizo .
inomboro yokutloliswa nayikuthi umkhiqizo sele utlolisiwe .

iincwadi zokuvuma nayikuthi imvumo ebuya emnikazini wokutlolisa iyafuneka ( imvumo yokutloliswa okususelwe esinonisini esikhona namkha imvumo yokusebenzisa igama lomkhiqizo wenye ikhampani elebuleni ) .
imali ebhadelwako elungileko .
amatjhege athunyelwa ngokwahlukana nesibawo kufanele aphekelelwe yincwadi ehlathululako ( amatjhege namaposoda oda kufanele enziwe abhadele u General : Agriculture ( umNqophisi wezokuLima ) .
isitifikeyidi sokucozulula namkha ikhasi ledatha . .

Amaforomo weembawo kufanele alethwe ngeduplikheyithi azaliswe ngokuzeleko , ngaphandle kokuqala iimbawo ezidlulileko , iinomboro zamakhasi namkha eminye imikhiqizo ( ubuncani bakhona yikhophi yinye yamaforomo weembawo okufanele ibe netlikitlo lamambala . .
Enye kungaba yikhophi ) . .

Amalungelo wabazalanisi beentjalo anikelwa kiyo yoke imihlobo yeentjalo evezwe ngokuya komThetho wamaLungelo womZalanisi weenTjalo ka . .
Pheze mihlobo ema yeentjalo efakwe erhemeni leentjalo ( Ithebula 1 ) okunganikelwa ngayo amalungelo wabazalanisi . .
UmTlolisi wamaLungelo wabaZalanisi beenTjalo angatjheja umhlobo njengomutjha abe anikele ngamalungelo wabazalanisi beentjalo nayikuthi : .
Into ezalisa ngokwemvelo yalowo mhlobo ayikathengiswa eSewula Afrika ukudlula umnyaka munye . .
Ebujameni bomhlobo womuthi namkha umuthi okhula ngokukhwela , into ezalisako ebe ingatholakali kwenye inarha , ekurhwebelaneni namkha emphakathini iminyaka edlula esithandathu , namkha ebujameni besitjalo , iminyaka edlula kwemine . .
Into ezalisa ngokwemvelo kufanele ikhambisane neemfuno ze ( ukwehluka , ukufana nokunzinza ) : .
kufanele ihlukaniswe ngokucacileko kweminye imihlobo efanako .
kufanele ifane , okutjho bona , zoke iintjalo endaweni yokutjala kufanele ziqaleke zifana begodu ezinesibumbeko esifanako .
kufanele zinzinze , okutjho bona , iintjalo zomhlobo othileko kufanele , ngemva kokutjala kanengana , zibonakale njengeentjalo zokuthoma .
kufanele zibe negama elamukelekako . .
Funda iThebula 1 yomThetho wamaLungelo womZalanisi weenTjalo ka ukuqinisekisa bona umhlobo wesitjalo walomhlobo okufuneka uvikelwe , uveziwe na . .
Nayikuthi umhlobo wesitjalo awukho ethebuleni , letha isibawo sokuvezwa nebanga ngomtlolo emTlolisini wamaLungelo wabaZalanisi beenTjalo . .
Nayikuthi umhlobo wesitjalo usethebuleni , okulandelako kufanele kulethwe : .
iforomo lesibawo elizaliswe ngokuzeleko .
iphephamibuzo lesithekhniki .
imali ebhadelwako ebekiweko kanye nemali yokuhlola .
imbewu namkha into ezalisa ngokwemvelo .
isigunyazo esitloliweko esibuya kumnikazi , nayikuthi awukazalanisi , wakhetha namkha wathuthukisa umhlobo . .
Veza ngokucacileko ephepheni lesithekhniki bona umhlobo omutjha uzakuhlolwa ngokumadaniswa namuphi umhlobo owaziwako khona kuzakufunyanwa umehluko . .
Ungenza isibawo sokuvikelwa kwesikhatjhana komhlobo . .
Lokhu kutjho bona umhlobo uvikelwe isikhathi soke sokulinganiswa , kufanele unikele isibopho esitloliweko sokobana angeze wathengisa ( ngaphandle kweminqopho yokwandisa namkha ukuhlola ) enye nenye into yokuzalanisa ngokwemvelo yomhlobo okukhulunywa ngawo bekufike lapho koke ukuhlola kuqedwa khona begodu kunikelwa amalungelo womzalanisi weentjalo . .
Ukuvikelwa kwesikhatjhana kuphakanyiswa eentjalweni lapho ukuhlola kuthatha isikhathi esidlula umnyaka munye . .
Kunamalanga abekiweko ngawo imitlolo nokuzizalela ngokwemvelo kufanele ilethwe kumTlolisi . .
Amalanga la , ubunengi bezinto zokuzizalela ngokwemvelo okufanele zithunyelwe begodu nalapho kufanele zilethwe emTlolisini , zitholakala ngesibawo kumTlolisi . .
Nayikuthi irhemo lemihlobo likhona kilowo mhlobo wesitjalo owenzelwa isibawo samalungelo womzalanisi , letha kanye kanye iimbawo ukubulunga isikhathi nemali . .
Koke ukudla kwefuyo okulethwa , okwenziwa , okukhiqizwa namkha okuthengiswa eSewula Afrika kufanele kutloliswe nomTlolisi . .

Ikhampani yangaphetjheya ayikavunyelwa ukuzitlolisa eSewula Afrika . .
Yikhampani kuphela yeSewula Afrika , isakhamuzi seSewula Afrika namkha ihlangano yangokomthetho eSewula Afrika engenza isibawo sokutloliswa kokudla kwefuyo neenonisi . .
Ukudla kwefuyo akufaki iinhlanga , i , ihoyi engakagaywa , ifurusibijwa , enye nenye ithoro namkha okhunye nokhunye ukudla umlimi akulingiselela ukukusebenzisa . .
Bawa imihlahlandlela ngeemfuno mazombe zokudla kwefuyo emTlolisini ( u , Act 36 of 1947 ) . .
Isibawo sokutloliswa kokudla kwefuyo sibunjwa : .
Yincwadi ephekelela isibawo ebuya emnikazini wokutlolisa namkha umjameli okhonjiweko . .
Incwadi ephekelela isibawo kufanele ifake : .
igama lomkhiqizo .
inomboro yokutloliswa nayikuthi umkhiqizo sele utlolisiwe .
ibanga lokulethwa ( nanyana sisitjha , isibawo sokutjhugululwa , isibawo sokutloliswa komkhiqizo osukela komunye ) .
iincwadi zemvumo nayikuthi imvumo ebuya kumnikazi wokutloliswa iyafuneka ( imvumo yokutloliswa komkhiqizo osukela komunye namkha imvumo yokusebenzisa igama lomkhiqizo wenye ikhampani eliselebuleni ) .
imali ebhadelwako elungileko .
amatjhege athunyelwa ngokuhlukana nesibawo kufanele aphekelelwe yincwadi ehlathululako . .
Amatjhege namaposoda kufanele enziwe abhadele u : Director : Agriculture . .
Letha amaforomo ( ngeduplikheyithi ) wesibawo weembawo ezitjha namatjhuguluko ekutlolisweni kwanjesi , kufaka indlela yokwenziwa kwetjhuguluko . .
Zalisa ngokuzeleko , ngaphandle kokukhuluma ngeembawo ezidlulileko , iinomboro zamakhasi namkha eminye imikhiqizo ( ubuncani bakhona ikhophi yinye yamaforomo wokutlolisa kufanele ibe namatlikitlo wamambala . .
Enye ingaba yikhophi ) . .
Amaforomo wesibawo kufanele atlikitlwe mumuntu okhethwe ngokomthetho begodu lokhu kunyulwa bona kube mumuntu othintana nomTlolisi nekhampani . .
Igama nenomboro yokutloliswa komkhiqizo kufanele isetjenziswe njengombana kutjhiwo esitifikeyidini sokutloliswa . .
Elinye nelinye itjhuguluko egameni , nanyana lilincani kangangani , lizakuthathwa njengetjhuguluko . .
Amaforomo weembawo kufanele alethwe e lezokuphatha . .
Ukunikela iimbawo kubaYelelisi besiThekniki kuzakuriyadisa ikambiso . .
Ukuthiya iimfesi ngomnqopho wokuzithabisa sisenzo esikhambelana neemfesi esifana nokuletha ngenarheni iimfesi ngeminqopho yokuzithabisa . .
Ukuletha ngenarheni iimfesi eziphila ngemanzini ngomnqopho wokuzithabisa , kufanele wenze isibawo semvumo yokuletha ngenarheni sokuzithabisa enikelwa nguNgqongqotjhe weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha namkha ngabasemagunyeni abavunyelweko . .
Iimfesi ezilethwa ngenarheni kufuze zingathengiswa kodwana kube zizokudliwa namkha zisetjenziswe nguwe . .
Akunamuntu ozakuletha ngenarheni iimfesi zelwandle ngaphandle kwemvumo yokuletha ngenarheni ngomnqopho wokuzithabisa . .
Yenza isibawo semvumo yokuletha ngenarheni ngeminqopho wokuzithabisa lokha ekhona nayiphelako . .
Ukubhalelwa kukhambisana nobujamo bemvumo kungaba nomphumela wokujanyiswa namkha wokusulwa kwayo . .
TJHEJA : Imvumo yokuletha ngenarheni ngomnqopho wokuzithabisa ayifaki iimfesi ezilawulwa mNyango wezokuLima . .
Iimbawo zemvumo yokuletha ngenarheni iimfesi eziphilako ezitholakala elwandle namkha iimfesi ze kufanele zenziwe begodu zinikelwe mNyango wezokuLima . .
Imibandela yeqintelo elandelako yokuletha ngenarheni iyasebenza : .
Akunamihlobo yeenlwanyana erhenyiswe ku ezakulethwa ngenarheni . .
( Nawufuna ilwazi elinabileko nge of International Trade in Endangered Species ( CITES ) , vakatjhela i ) . .
IimVumo zokuLetha ngeNarheni ezikhutjhelwa ukuletha ngenarheni iimfesi ozazisebenzisa namkha uzidle wena zizakusebenza isikhathi sekhambo lokuya nokubuya enarheni leyo . .
Akunamfesi zelwandle eziphilako ezizakulethwa ngenarheni . .
Zalisa amaforomo weembawo afaneleko begodu uwalethe emNyangweni weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha kanye nelwazi elilandelako : .
amalanga wokusuka nokubuya eSewula Afrika .
igama lenarha evakatjhelwako .
yitjho umkhawulo weSewula Afrika enizakungena kiwo nanibuyela eSewula Afrika .
ubufakazi be yomakho , inomboro yokuthintana neenomboro zefeksi eSewula Afrika .
yitjho bona iimfesi zizakulethwa njani ngenarheni ( Zikghadzisiwe / Ziqandiswe zizitjha ) .
ikhophi eqinisekisiweko yencwadi yokuzazisa yomunye nomunye umbawi . .
ubufakazi bokubhadela ( isilibhu sebhanga semali ebhadelwako eyi umbawi ngamunye ) .
akunamafeksi , amakhophi nama azakwamukelwa .
amaforomo angalethwa ngesandla , ngeposo namkha ngefeksi . .
Sibawa utjheje : .
Yenza isibawo ubuncani bakhona iimveke ezimbili ngaphambi kokukhamba ukuvumela ukusetjenzwa kwesibawo . .
Akunamvumo ezokufuneka nawufuna ukuletha ukudla kokuthiya . .
Kodwana , sibawa uqinisekise bona uphethe imvumo yokudla kokuthiya ngomnqopho wokuzithabisa ( kuphela nayikuthi iqintelo lomthwalo lingathuthwa ) namkha isilibhu sekhetjhe ekudleni kokuthiya okuthengiweko . .
Ukuthiya iimfesi ngomnqopho wokwenza imali sisenzo esikhambelana nokuthiya iimfesi esifana nokuthumela ngaphandle iimfesi ngeminqopho yokurhwebelana . .
Ukuthumela ngaphandle okuphila ngemanzini eenarheni zangaphandle namkha ngaphandle kwemikhawulo yeRiphabliki yeSewula Afrika , kufuze wenze isibawo semvumo yokuthumela ngaphandle enikelwa nguNgqongqotjhe weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha namkha ngabasemagunyeni abavunyelweko . .
Akunamuntu ovunyelwe ukuthumela ngaphandle iimfesi ngaphandle kwemvumo . .
Lokha imvumo yokuthumela ngaphandle ekhona nayiphela ngemva kwenyanga ezintathu , kufuze wenze isibawo semvumo etjha . .
Ukubhalelwa kukhambisana nobujamo bemvumo kungaba nomphumela wokujanyiswa namkha wokusulwa kwayo . .
TJHEJA : Imvumo yokuthumela ngaphandle iimfesi ayifaki iimfesi ezilawulwa mNyango wezokuLima . .
Iimbawo zemvumo yokuthumela ngaphandle zeemfesi ezingatholakali elwandle namkha iimfesi ze kufuze zenziwe emNyangweni wezokuLima . .
Imihlobo erhenyiswe mHlangano weenTjhabatjhaba wokuRhwebelana ngeenLwanyana eziseNgozini yokuTjhabalala akukafaneli ilethwe ngenarheni . .
( Nawufuna ilwazi elinabileko nge of International Trade in Endangered Species ( CITES ) , vakatjhela i ) .
ImVumo yokuThumela ngaPhandle ekhutjhelwa imihlobo ye kufuze iphekelelwe sitifikeyidi se komunye nomunye umthwalo . .
IimVumo zokuThumela ngaPhandle ezikhutjhelwa i tuna , i bluefish tuna , i , i toothfish kanye ne toothfish kufuze ziphekelelwe mtlolo weembalo wokubanjwa ofaneleko komunye nomunye umthwalo . .
Imitlolo yeembalo zokubanjwa itholakala emNyangweni weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha , iGatja : Marine and Coastal Management , Directorate : Offshore and High Seas Fisheries Management . .
Yenza isibawo semvumo yokuthumela ngaphandle . .
Fumana amaforomo wesibawo sokuthumela ngaphandle kanye neforomo lesibawo se e le and Coastal Management ( qala imininingwana yokuthintana ngenzasi ) namkha e legatja lomNyango weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha namkha likhuphe kwa . .
Funda iforomo lesibawo kuhle begodu wenze isiqiniseko sokobana wanelisa iimfuno zesibawo kanye nobujamo . .
Nikela ngelwazi elilandelako : .
ama womakho woletha ngenarheni enarheni okuthunyelwa kiyo .
amagama ajayelekileko newamambala wemihlobo ezakuthunyelwa ngaphandle .
ubungako bemihlobo ezakuthunyelwa ngaphandle .
ebujameni lapho umsebenzeli athinteka khona , isivumelwano phakathi kwababili kufuze sinanyathiselwe kanye namakhophi wama wabatlikitli .
amakhophi wemitlolo yeembalo zokubanjwa kufuze anikelwe kiyo yoke i tuna , i bluefish tuna , i , i toothfish kanye ne toothfish ethunyelwa ngaphandle ngaphasi kwemvumo yokuthumela ngaphandle edlulileko . .
Nayikuthi umbawi wemvumo yokuthumela ngaphandle akasi mnikazi welungelo lokuthiya , nikela ngemitlolo elandelako : .
ubufakazi bokunikela kanye nama womakho wabanikeli beemfesi zelwandle ezizakuthunyelwa ngaphandle .
amagama ajayelekileko newamambala wemihlobo ezakuthunyelwa ngaphandle .
ubungako bemihlobo ezakuthunyelwa ngaphandle . .

incwadi yokuzazisa ( i ) nemitlolo yokuzitlolisa yekhampani yakho , i corporation namkha i .
iimvumo ezisebenzako zokuthumela ngaphandle ezibuya emNyangweni wezokuRhwebelana namaBubulo namkha izaziso zeemvumo .

Ukuletha ngenarheni iimfesi ngomnqopho wokwenza imali kutjho ukwenza izenzo ezifana nokuletha ngenarheni iimfesi zelwandle ngeminqopho yokurhwebelana . .
Ukuletha ngenarheni iimfesi eziphila ngemanzini , kufuze wenze isibawo semvumo yokuletha ngenarheni enikelwa nguNgqongqotjhe weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha ( okuyi ) namkha ngabasemagunyeni abavunyelweko . .
Akunamuntu ovunyelwe ukuletha ngenarheni iimfesi eziphila elwandle ngaphandle kwemvumo . .
Yenza isibawo semvumo etjha yokuletha ngenarheni lokha ekhona nayiphelako . .
Ukubhalelwa kukhambisana nobujamo bemvumo kungaba nomphumela wokujanyiswa namkha wokusulwa kwayo . .
TJHEJA : Lemvumo yokuletha ngenarheni ayifaki iimfesi ezilawulwa mNyango wezokuLima . .
Iimbawo zemvumo yokuletha ngenarheni zeemfesi ezingatholakali elwandle namkha iimfesi ze kufuze zenziwe emNyangweni wezokuLima . .
Amaqintelo wokuletha ngenarheni alandelako ayasebenza : .
Imihlobo erhenyiswe mHlangano weenTjhabatjhaba wokuRhwebelana ngeenLwanyana eziseNgozini yokuTjhabalala ( i ) akukafaneli ilethwe ngenarheni . .
( Nawufuna ilwazi elinabileko nge of International Trade in Endangered Species ( CITES ) , vakatjhela i ) .
ImVumo yokuletha ngenarheni ekhutjhelwa imihlobo ye , ama lobster kanye nemihlobo ebekwe emThethweni wemiThombo yangeLwandle ePhilako ka ( umthetho 18 ka ) ( The Marine Living Resources Act , 1998 ( Act 18 of 1998 ) ) isiNgezelelo 4,5 , no , izakusebenza komunye nomunye umthwalo ( iimveke ezintathu ukusuka ngelanga lokukhutjhwa ) . .
Ma akghadzisiweko kuphela ( namkha iinquntu zawo ) anobudisi obuyi namkha ukudlula lapho ngayinye kanye namatoni angadluli ama angalethwa ngenarheni ( ngomnyaka ) . .
Akuna ephilako engalethwa ngenarheni . .
Fumana iforomo lesibawo sokuletha ngenarheni ngokuthumela isibawo e le and Coastal Management ( qala imininingwana yokuthintana ngenzasi ) namkha egatjeni le lomNyango weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha namkha likhuphe kwa . .
Funda iforomo lesibawo kuhle begodu wenze isiqiniseko sokobana wanelisa iimfuno zesibawo kanye nobujamo . .
Nikela ngelwazi elilandelako : .
ama womakho wabathumela ngaphandle ngenarheni okusula kiyo umthwalo .
amagama ajayelekileko newamambala wemihlobo .
ubungako bemihlobo ezakulethwa ngenarheni . .
Letha isibawo sakho nemitlolo elandelako : .
ikhophi eqinisekisiweko yencwadi yokuzazisa ( i ) nemitlolo yokuzitlolisa yekhampani yakho , i corporation namkha i .
amakhophi aqinisekisiweko weemvumo ezisebenzako zokuletha ngenarheni ezibuya emNyangweni wezokuRhwebelana namaBubulo namkha izaziso zeemvumo ( i ) .
amakhophi aqinisekisiweko wamambala weenTifikeyidi zokuVunyelwa zomThelo ezivunywe bezakhutjhwa yi African Revenue Service ( i ) . .

Ikhampani ezitlolisa ngobunikazi bezabelo ( imali yokuthoma ) kumele ithumele imitlolo elandelako : .
CM1 : Isitifikeyidi sokufakwa .
Lokhu kumtlolo otlikitlwa bewugadangiswe isitembu mTlolisi wamaKhampani lapho imitlolo ekhambisanako ( erheliswe ngaphezulu ) seyiqalisisiwe bekwaqedwa ngayo . .
I : Imemorandamu of association kanye ne- CM2A - CM2B - CM2C nangabe abanikazi bezabelo badlula munye namkha u nangabe munye umnikazi wezabelo . .
UmThetho wemiTjhado yesiNtu waba mthetho ngomhlaka 15 Novemba 2000 . .
Nayikuthi bewungaphasi komtjhado wanjesi osebenzako ngaphasi komthetho wesintu ngaphambi kwelanga leli , umtjhado wakho uyavunywa ngaphasi kwalomthetho omutjha . .
Lokha umyeni sele anokosikazi odlula munye , yoke imitjhado iyavunywa ngaphasi kwalomthetho omutjha . .
LomThetho godu uvuma imitjhado yesintu eyenziwe ngaphambi kwalelilanga begodu ubeka imithetho abantu abatjhada ngaphasi komthetho wesintu okufanele bayilandele khona imitjhado yabo izakuvunywa . .
Umtjhado wesintu uyavunywa nayikuthi abantu abatjhada ngaphasi komthetho wesintu bakhambisene neemfuno ezilandelako : .
Bobabili abathinteka emtjhadweni kufanele babe neminyaka engaphezulu kweli . .
Bobabili abathintekako kufanele bavume ukutjhada ngaphasi komthetho wesintu . .
Umtjhado kufanele kukhulunyiswane ngawo , uthatjelwe bewenziwe ngokuya komthetho wesintu . .
Amalobolo awasi yinto etlhogekako ekusebenzeni komtjhado wesintu . .
Tjheja bona imitjhado le ihlala ivunywa ngaphasi komthetho wesintu . .
Ngifanele kutlolisa umtjhado wami nini ? .
Nayikuthi wawutjhade ngaphasi komthetho wesintu ngaphambi komhlaka 15 Novemba 2000 , umtjhado wakho kufanele utloliswe nomNyango weeNdaba zeKhaya . .
Nayikuthi wawutjhade ngemva kokuphasiswa komthetho , kufanele utlolise umtjhado wakho kungakapheli iinyanga ezintathu ngemva komtjhado . .
ImiTjhado yesiNtu nokutjhada ngokuHlanganyela iPahla .
Yoke imitjhado yesintu eyenziwa ngemva kokuthoma ukusebenza komThetho iba ngeyokuhlanganyela ipahla . .
Lokhu kutjho bona umyeni nokosikazi banesabelo esilinganako epahleni , imali begodu lokhu kutjho bona babelana ngazo zoke iinkolodo . .
Nayikuthi abathintekako bangathanda bona umtjhado wabo ube ngewokungahlanganyeli ipahla kuzakufanela bona benze isivumelwano sangaphambi komtjhado mayelana nokwabiwa kwepahla ( i contract ) . .
Nabafuna ukusitjhugulula ngemva kobana sele batjhadile kuzakufanela bona benze isibawo eKhotho ePhakamileko . .
Ngaphasi komThetho wemiTjhado yesiNtu ukosikazi unelungelo nobujamo obulingana nebakababa ukuqunta bona kwenzekani epahleni . .
Ukosikazi othethwe isintu unekghono lokwenza iimvumelwano ngaphandle kwerhelebho lakababa . .
Kwenzekani nayikuthi umyeni wami ufuna ukutjhada omunye ukosikazi ? .
Umyeni kufanele enze isivumelwano esitloliweko / ikontraga ezakubeka bona ngikuphi okufanele kwenzeke epahleni begodu umyeni uzakwenza isibawo ekhotho sokuvunywa kwesivumelwano esitloliweko . .
Ikhotho kufanele iqinisekise bona yoke ipahla yabo boke abokosikazi iyavikelwa . .
Kwenzekani nayikuthi sifuna ukwenza umtjhado ongafuni isondo ngemva komtjhado wesintu ? .
Nayikuthi umyeni wakho akanabanye abokosikazi , ungatjhada ngaphasi komthetho womtjhado ongafuni isondo kanye nomthetho wesintu . .
Kodwana , akunamunye phakathi kwenu ozakukghona ukwenza imitjhado yesintu nomunye umuntu ngesikhathi nitjhade ngaphasi komthetho womtjhado ongafuni isondo . .
Wena namkha umyenakho angazitlolisa e eliseduze lomNyango weeNdaba zeKhaya . .
Kuyeleliswa bona bobabili abathintekako baye bobabili ukutlolisa umtjhado wabo khona bazakurhabisa ukutloliswa . .
Kodwana , nayikuthi omunye othethene naye uyabhala , ungatlolisa ngokwakho bewulethe ubufakazi obufaneleko . .
Letha incwadi kamazisi ( i ) begodu zalisa iForomo A : Application for registration / enquiry into existence of customary marriage ( Isibawo sokutloliswa / ukubuza ngomtjhado wesintu okhona ) elifuna bona ubeke ilwazi elilandelako : .
iinomboro zabomazisi ( i ) , amagama namalanga wamabeletho womyeni nokosikazi .
igama lababelethi bomyeni nokosikazi kanye negama lomrholi wendabuko .
imininingwana yesivumelwano samalobolo / magadi , kanye .
nabantu ababofakazi emtjhadweni ( munye ufakazi kufanele ajamele umyeni kuthi omunye ajamele ukosikazi ) .
incwadi ebuya emrholini wendabuko namkha isifungo . .
Iforomo kufanele liqinisekiswe belitlikitlwe phambi : .
kwesiphathiswa sokutlolisa , namkha .
umuntu okhonjiweko , okhonjwe ngokunjalo Mnqophisi ukwenza imisebenzi ngokuya kwemithetjhwana . .
Isibawo kufanele senziwe esiphathisweni sokutlolisa namkha umuntu okhonjiweko okufanele akunikele irasidi lokuvuma ukufumana isibawo eForomini B : Acknowledgement of receipt of application for registration of customary marriage ( Ukuvuma ukufunyanwa kwesibawo sokutloliswa komtjhado wesintu ) .
Isiphathiswa sokutlolisa namkha umuntu okhonjiweko uzakudlulisela phambili isibawo e eliseduze lesifunda namkha lesiyingi lomNyango bona sifakwe erejisteni yokutloliswa kwesitjhaba . .
Uzakunikelwa isitifikeyidi sokutloliswa namkha iForomo C : Customary marriage certificate ( Isitifikeyidi somtjhado wesintu ) . .
Gcina isitifikeyidi endaweni ephephileko ngombana siqakathekile . .
Isikepe sangaphandle sokuthiya sikepe umnikazi waso ongasi sisakhamuzi seSewula Afrika , isibonelo , iphandle begodu nesitloliswe ngaphasi kweNarha eNye ngaphandle kweRiphabhliki yeSewula Afrika . .
Kungakaphasi kobujamo obungakajayeleki lapho isikepe singaqatjhiswa namkha sikontragiswe mNikazi weLungelo weSewula Afrika ukwenza imisebenzi yokuthiya ngaphakathi kwe Economic Zone ( EEZ ) namkha emanzini weentjhabatjhaba awela ngaphasi kwelawulo leSewula Afrika . .
Akunasikepe sangaphandle esizakunikelwa ilayisense yokuthiya yeSewula Afrika ngaphandle kwalokha nasithiya ngokuhlanganyela nomNikazi weLungelo weSewula Afrika . .
Ngaphambi kokwenza imisebenzi yokuthiya , umNyango weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha kufuze uthintwe ukuqunta ukobana ukuqatjhwa kwesikepe sangaphandle kuzakuvunyelwa na ekorweni yokuthiya ethileko begodu nokuthi ngimiphi imitlolo efuneka ekuvunyweni kwesibawo esinjalo . .
Nayikuthi isekelo langokomthetho linikelwa ukusetjenziswa kwesikepe sangaphandle umbawi kufuneka afumane iforomo lelayisense yesikepe sangaphandle e eliseduze lomNyango weeNdaba zeBhoduluko nezokuVakatjha . .
Zalisa iforomo lesibawo begodu ulilethe e eliseduze le of Environmental Affairs and Tourism ( DEAT ) nelwazi elilandelako : .
igama lesikepe sokuthiya .
igama nemininingwana yomnikazi wesikepe ( kufaka ubunikazi bezabelo nayikuthi ngesezakhamizi zeSewula Afrika ) .
amandla wenjini yesikepe .
ubude nobukhulu besikepe .
inomboro yokutloliswa yesikepe .
inarha ngaphasi kwayo isikepe esitloliswe kiyo ( nayikuthi siqatjhisiwe namkha ngokuhlanganyela ngesezakhamizi zeSewula Afrika .
isitifikeyidi sezokuphepha esisebenzako esibuya enarheni esitloliswe kiyo isikepe . .
Isikepe sokuthiya sizakuhlolelwa ukufaneleka kukuba selwandle yi African Maritime Safety Authority iindleko zakho ezizakubhadelwa mnikazi . .
Zoke iinkepe zangaphandle kufuneka bona zibe ne C VMS esebenzako ebikela i and Coastal Management . .
Lokhu kufuze kuqinisekiswe liPhiko lokuSebenza le le and Coastal Management . .
Esibaweni sakho , veza ikoro yokuthiya isikepe esizakufakwa kiyo kanye nesikhathi esizasiqeda lapho . .
Incwadi yangokomthetho ebuya kubaPhathi bezokuThiya beNarha isikepe esiTlolise ngaPhasi Kwayo ( i State's Fisheries Authority ) izakufuneka , evuma bonyana : .
isikepe sivunyelwe ukuthiya emanzini weSewula Afrika .
isikepe asikafunyanwa senza imisebenzi yokuthiya eNgakavunyelwa , eNgalawulwako neNgakabikwa .
i State's Fisheries Authority izakuthatha isibopho sokuphatha isikepe .
i State's Fisheries Authority izakuthatha isibopho sokubika ngokubamba eenHlanganweni zesiFunda eziQalene nokuPhathwa kokuBanjwa kweemFesi ( okuyi Fisheries Management Organisations ( i ) nayikuthi kuyafuneka .
Ngokuya kwe zoke iimbalo zokubanjwa kweemfesi , kungaqalwa bona zibanjwe e yeSewula Afrika namkha emaLwandle aPhakamileko , kuzakuba ngekweSewula Afrika bekuphele isivumelwano sokuqatjhisa .
isikepe sangaphandle sizakuthiya ngaphasi kwemithetjhwana yeSewula Afrika nobujamo bemvumo . .
Nayikuthi isikepe akusi ngesikhethiweko ngokuya kwekambiso yokwabiwa kwamalungelo , umbawi kufuneka azalise iforomo lokudluliswa kwesikepe . .
Nakuzakugunyazwa isikepe bona sithiye umbawi kufuze azalise iforomo lesibawo khona azakufumana imvumo yokuthiya ngokuya kwekoro isikepe esithiya kiyo . .
Kokugcina , nayikuthi umbawi ubona ungathi isikepe naso sizakuthiya emaLwandle aPhakamileko ngesikhathi sokuqatjhiswa , iforomo lesibawo samaLwandle aPhakamileko nalo kufuneka lizaliswe . .
