Isinghonghoyilo seHlangothi IV : Singhonghoyilo esisola bona ilunga lenze isenzo sokwephula umthetho ngaphandle kwalezo ezirhenyiswe ngehla namkha ukungaziphathi kuhle okungakhenge kube nomphumela wokuhlongakala namkha ukulimala kumbi komunye . .
Isinghonghoyilo seHlangothi V : Singhonghoyilo esenzeka ngaphandle kwegunya namkha lomthethomgomo we . .
Iinghonghoyilo ezingeze zenziwa kwa : .
Iinghonghoyilo zezehlakalo ezenzeka ngaphambi kokuhlonywa kwe . .
Lokhu kutjho zoke izehlakalo ezenzeka ngaphambi kokuhlonywa kwe . .
Lokhu kutjho zoke izehlakalo ezenzeka ngaphambi komhlaka Apreli 1997 kanye nalezo ezenzeka esikhathini esidlula umnyaka ngaphambi kobana zibikwe kwa , ngaphandle kobana kube nobujamo obunye . .
Iinghonghoyilo ezenziwa ngabasebenzi bemiSebenzi yokuLungiswa kokuziPhatha ( okuyi Services ) , iinkhulu zekhotho kanye namalunga wamaJoni weSewula Afrika . .
Amagadango okufanele alandelwe .
Ungenza isinghonghoyilo ngokwakho , ngomtato , ngencwadi namkha nge e eliseduze le . .
Iinghonghoyilo zingenziwa ngesikhathi somsebenzi , phakathi kwaka no . .
Zalisa iForomo lokuBika isiNghonghoyilo ( i Reporting Form ) ( Form 1 ) bewulifeksele e eliseduze le . .
I ingakubawa ukunikela ngelwazi elingezelelweko ngaphambi kobana isinghonghoyilo siphenywe . .
Nayikuthi uza ngokwakho , uzakubonana nesisebenzi esiphethe umlandu namkha umcozululi . .
Lapho umuntu arhola ingeniso engaweli ngaphasi kokudoswa kwe namkha i ( isibonelo , inzuzo , irende namkha ingeniso yebhizinisi ) , kufanele abhadele umthelo kasolanga ngale ngeniso . .
Ukubhadelwa komthelo kasolanga kwenziwa esikhathini esiziinyanga ezisithandathu . .
Umthelo kasolanga uhlose ukurhelebha ababhadela umthelo ukuhlangabezana neenkolodo esikhathini esilandelanako kunokobana babhadele imali enengi kanye ngomnyaka ngesikhathi sokuhlolwa . .
Umthelo kasolanga obhadelwako uzakususelwa emthelweni wengeniso wokugcina ( umthelo ojayelekileko ) umuntu okufanele awubhadele emnyakeni wokuhlola ofaneleko . .
Umuntu okoloda ukubhadela umthelo kasolanga kufanele kungakapheli amalanga ama wokukoloda , enze isibawo ngomtlolo sokutloliswa e legatja le African Revenue Service ( SARS ) . .
Ukubhalelwa kukwenza njalo kuzakuba nomphumela wenzuzo nehlawulo ekubhadeleni kwangemva kwesikhathi kokulethwa sekudlule isikhathi kwamaforomo . .
Ilanga lokugicna lokubhadelwa komthelo kasolanga sikhathi esiziinyanga ezisithandathu zokuthoma komnyaka wokuhlola . .
Ukubhadelwa komthelo kasolanga kufanele kujamele isiquntu sesikolo somthelo somnyaka ozeleko wokuthelisa . .
Balisisa umthelo kasolanga ngendlela elandelako esikhathini sokuthoma : .
isiquntu somthelo woke womnyaka ozeleko .
umthelo womsebenzi omncani odoswa esikhathini lesi ( iinyanga ezisithandathu ) .
imali yerhelebho encani evunyelwa emthelweni esikhathini lesi ( iinyanga ezisithandathu ) . .
Bhadela ngesaziso esibekiweko se ngomhlaka namkha ngaphambi kwamalanga wokugcina wokubhadela . .
I izakuthumelela ababhadela umthelo abazitlolisileko amaforomo afaneleko . .
Iindlela ezilandelako zokubhadela i ziyatholakala : .
ukubhadelwa komthelo wesikhatjhana kungenziwa kwelinye nelinye i legatja le , ngoMvulo ukufika ngeLesihlanu phakathi kwaka no , kungafaki amalanga womphakathi wokuphumula .
lapho ukubhadela kwenziwa ngeposo , ngokusebenzisa ibhanka namkha i- ATM , isikhathi esaneleko sokuposa namkha sokusetjenzwa kufanele siyelelwe .
lapho ukubhadela kwenziwa ngokwe , kufanele kuqalelelwe isikhathi sokuqintelwa sebhanga yakho kanye nesikhathi sokuvunyelwa esingathatha amalanga aphakathi kwamabili ukuya kwamahlanu . .
Imininingwana yebhanga : .
Amatlayenti abhadela ekhawunthareni kwelinye nelinye igatja le , le , namkha le angeze kusatlhogeka bona anikele ngenomboro ye yebhanga kanye nekhowudu yebhanga lokha nawabhadelako . .
Lokhu kusebenza ngokulingana kiwo woke amatlayenti abhanka nge we , i , i , kanye ne Bank . .
Ozakufuneka yi : .
nomboro yetlayendi yereferensi yokubhadela eneenomboro ezili ; kanye .
nenomboro yokuzazisa yomzuzi / ye ehlanganiswe nomhlobo othileko womthelo ukubhadela . .
Imininingwana le itjengiswe emtlolweni wobufakazi bokubhadela beforomo le 6 . .
Nayikuthi ilanga lokugcina lokubhadela liwela ngaphasi kwelanga lokuphumula namkha lepelaveke , ukubhadela kufanele kwenziwe ngelanga lokugcina lokusebenza elingaphambi kwelanga lokuphumula namkha lepelaveke . .
Nawufuna imininingwana ezeleko qala iwebhusayidi ye kwa .
Tjheja : .
Amaforomo we 6 wesikhathi sokuthoma kufanele alethwe nanyana ngokuya kokubalisisa , akunamthelo obhadelwako . .
Nayikuthi ukubhadelwa komthelo kasolanga kusekelwe engenisweni etheliswako elinganisiweko engaphasi kwenani elisisekelo , isibawo nebanga kufanele kufakwe . .
Iforomo le 6 lesikhathi sokuthoma manje litjengisa isikhala lapho kufanele ufake ibanga lesibawo esinjalo . .
Nayikuthi i ayaneliswa isilinganiso esibuyekeziweko singabawiwa . .
Ukubalekela ihlawulo nenzuzo , yenza isiqiniseko sokobana amaforomo we 6 alethwa e legatja le elifaneleko ngaphambi kwelanga lokugcina lokubhadela . .
Lokhu kuzakuqinisekisa bona isibawo sakho siyafunyanwa begodu sisetjenzwa ngesikhathi . .
Isiquntu sesaziso sokubhadela seforomo le 6 manje sisekhasini elinye . .
Iforomo lakho ngalokho lingalethwa ngokuhlukana nokubhadela kwakho . .
Funda imiHlahlandlela ye IRP 12 Guidelines nayikuthi ufuna irhelebho ekuzaliseni iforomo le 6 . .
Lapho umuntu arhola ingeniso etheliswako engaweli ngaphasi kokudoswa kwe namkha i ( isibonelo , inzuzo , irende namkha ingeniso yebhizinisi ) , kufanele abhadele umthelo kasolanga ngale ngeniso . .
Ukubhadelwa komthelo kasolanga kwenziwa esikhathini esiziinyanga ezisithandathu . .
Umthelo kasolanga uhlose ukurhelebha ababhadela umthelo ukuhlangabezana neenkolodo zomthelo esikhathini esilandelanako kunokobana babhadele imali enengi kanye ngomnyaka ngesikhathi sokuhlolwa . .
Umthelo kasolanga obhadelwako uzakususelwa emthelweni wengeniso wokugcina ( umthelo ojayelekileko ) umuntu okufanele awubhadele emnyakeni wokuhlola ofaneleko . .
Umuntu okoloda ukubhadela umthelo kasolanga kufanele kungakapheli amalanga ama wokukoloda , enze isibawo ngomtlolo sokuzitlolisa e legatja le African Revenue Service ( SARS ) . .
Ukubhalelwa kukwenza njalo kuzakuba nomphumela wenzuzo nehlawulo ekubhadeleni kwangemva kwesikhathi ekulethweni sekudlule isikhathi kwamaforomo . .
Ilanga lokugcina lokubhadelwa komthelo kasolanga akusi ngemva kwelanga lokugcina lomnyaka wokuhlola namkha ilanga lokugcina elivunyiweko lomnyaka weemali . .
Tjheja : ( kusebenza kuphela ebantwini nama ) .
Lapho ukuphela konyaka weemali kaFebherbari kuletha ubudisi begodu ukuvunywa kufunyenwe kwa ukuletha iintatimende zeemali ngelanga elinye ngaphandle kokuphela kwakaFeberbari , abantu abanjalo godu bangabawa ukuvunywa kokuletha amaforomo womthelo kasolanga ngokukhambisana nokuphela komnyaka weemali ovunyiweko . .
Yoke enye ingeniso kodwana ihlala emnyakeni wokuhlola ophela ngomhlaka 28 / 29 Feberbari . .
Balisisa umthelo kasolanga ngendlela elandelako esikhathini sesibili : .
isamba soke somthelo olinganisiweko womnyaka ozeleko .
umthelo womsebenzi omncani obhadelwe umnyaka woke .
imali yerhelebho encani emakhredithini womthelo wangaphandle umnyaka woke .
imali encani ebhadelwa esikhathini sokuthoma . .
Bhadela ngesaziso esibekiweko seforomo IRP6 ngomhlaka namkha ngaphambi kwamalanga wokugcina wokubhadela . .
Iindlela ezilandelako zokubhadela i ziyatholakala : .
Ukubhadelwa komthelo wesikhatjhana kungenziwa kwelinye nelinye i legatja le , ngoMvulo ukufika ngeLesihlanu phakathi kwaka no , kungafaki amalanga womphakathi wokuphumula . .
Lapho ukubhadela kwenziwa ngeposo , ngokusebenzisa ibhanka namkha i- ATM , isikhathi esaneleko sokuposa namkha sokusetjenzwa kufanele siyelelwe . .
Lapho ukubhadela kwenziwa ngokwe , kufanele kuqalelelwe isikhathi sokuqintelwa sebhanga yakho kanye nesikhathi sokuvunyelwa esingathatha amalanga aphakathi kwamabili ukuya kwamahlanu . .
Imininingwana yebhanga : .
Amatlayenti abhadela ekhawunthareni kwelinye nelinye igatja le , le , namkha le angeze kusatlhogeka bona anikele ngenomboro ye yebhanga kanye nekhowudu yebhanga lokha nawabhadelako . .
Lokhu kusebenza ngokulingana kiwo woke amatlayenti abhanka nge we , i , i , kanye ne Bank . .
Ozakufuneka yi : .
nomboro yetlayendi yereferensi yokubhadela eneenomboro ezili .
nenomboro yokuzazisa yomzuzi / ye ehlanganiswe nomhlobo othileko womthelo ukubhadela . .
Imininingwana le itjengiswe emtlolweni wobufakazi bokubhadela beforomo le 6 . .
Ukubhadela okungakhambisani nenomboro yereferensi yokubhadela okukhulunywe ngayo ngehla kanye nenomboro yomzuzi yokuzazisa angeze kwamukelwa . .
Nayikuthi ilanga lokugcina lokubhadela liwela ngaphasi kwelanga lokuphumula namkha lepelaveke , ukubhadela kufanele kwenziwe ngelanga lokugcina lokusebenza elingaphambi kwelanga lokuphumula namkha lepelaveke . .
Tjheja : .
Amaforomo we 6 wesikhathi sesibili kufanele alethwe nanyana ngokuya kokubalisisa , kunganamthelo obhadelwako . .
Ukubhadelwa kwesibili komthelo kasolanga kufanele kusekelwe esilinganisweni sengeniso etheliswako esilingana nenani elisisekelo namkha inani lamambala lengeniso etheliswako yomnyaka loyo . .
Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana amaforomo we alethwa e legatja le kusese nesikhathi ngaphambi kwelanga lokugcina lokubhadela . .
Lokhu kuzakuqinisekisa bona isibawo sakho siyafunyanwa begodu sisetjenzwa ngesikhathi begodu awuzukubhadela iimali zehlawulo nenzuzo . .
Isiquntu sesaziso sokubhadela seforomo le 6 manje sisekhasini elinye . .
Iforomo lakho ngalokho lingalethwa ngokuhlukana nokubhadela kwakho . .
Funda imiHlahlandlela ye 12 Guidelines nayikuthi ufuna irhelebho ekuzaliseni iforomo le 6 . .
Irizeva lamapholisa lilunga lomphakathi elisebenza isikhathi esithileko ( ubuncani bakhona ama ali ngenyanga ) imisebenzi yesipholisa namkha imisebenzi ye African Police Service ( SAPS ) ngokuzinikela ngaphandle kokurhola . .
Uba lirizeva emahlangothini alandelako : .
I leHlangothi A - Ukusebenza kwesipholisa : .
lenza imisebenzi kiwo woke amahlangothi wokusebenza wesipholisa esitetjhini , ezingeni lendawo namkha lephrovinsi kodwana ingasi imisebenzi ekhethekileko .
lingambatha iyunifomo .
lizakubandula emahlangothini afaneleko wokusebenza kwesipholisa . .
IRizeva leHlangothi B - Imisebenzi yokusekela : .
lenza imisebenzi ethileko yokusekela ngakwezokuphatha ezingeni lesitjhaba , lephrovinsi namkha lesitetjhi begodu angeze lenza imisebenzi yokusebenza kwesipholisa .
alimbathi iyunifomo .
lapho kutlhogekako , lingabandulwa emahlangothini wezomthetho , umthethomgomo kanye nemilayo esebenza kilemisebenzi ethileko . .
IRizeva leHlangothi C - Ukusebenza okuthekileko kwesipholisa : .
kufanele libe namakghono athileko namkha ilemuko elingasetjenziswa ukusebenza siPholisa , isibonelo , abatjhayeli beemphaphamtjhini , abodorhodera , abasebenzi bezehlalakuhle namkha abasebenzi berhelebho lezengqondo .
lizakwenza imisebenzi ethileko ezikweni lalo lelemuko .
ngokuvuma kwakakhomanda lingambatha iyunifomo .
kufanele libandulwe emahlangothini afaneleko wezomthetho , umthethomgomo kanye nemilayo elisebenza ngayo . .
IRizeva leHlangothi D - Ikoro yesipholisa yemakhaya nemadorobheni : .
lenza imisebenzi yokusebenza kwesipholisa ekhambelana nekoro yesipholisa eendaweni zemakhaya nezemadorobheni ekorweni ethileko ezingeni lesitetjhi ; namkha lizakwenza kuphela imisebenzi eendaweni ezithileko ngaphakathi kwekoro ethileko njengokuqunta kwakakhomanda .
lingambatha iyunifomo kuye ngokusetjenziswa .
kufanele libandulwe emahlangothini afaneleko wekoro kanye / namkha nekusebenzeni kwesipholisa okukhambelana nemisebenzi yalo . .
Ibandulo elingezelelweko lingafuneka nayikuthi lizibandakanya emisebenzini yesipholisa yokusebenza kwekoro . .
Irizeva elikhonjelwe ihlangothi lokuthoma lingadluliselwa kwelinye ihlangothi nayikuthi likhambisana nazo zoke iimfuno zehlangothi elithileko begodu libandulwe namkha lifuna ukufumana ibandulo elifunekako kilelohlangothi . .
Ngokuya kwemithetjhwana ye African Reserve Police Service kufanele : .
ube sisakhamuzi sakanomphela seSewula Afrika .
ubuncani bakhona ube neminyaka eli begodu ube ngaphasi kweminyaka ema ubudala .
uzalise iphephamibuzo lezamaphilo njengokuqunta kwakaKomitjhinara wesiTjhaba .
ungabi nokugula ngokomkhumbulo , ubulwele namkha ukungakaqini emkhumbulweni namkha emzimbeni okungakuliya ekwenzeni kuhle imisebenzi yakho .
kube uziphethe kuhle , ngombana kufanele kubuzwe ngokuziphatha kwakho .
uphumelele ngepumelelo iinhlahlubo zengqondo namkha ukuhlolwa okuquntwe nguKomitjhinara wesiTjhaba wamaPholisa .
ubuncani bakhona ube nesitifikeyidi sebanga letjhumi namkha esilingana naso begodu ulethe ubufakazi baso bomtlolo ; .
ukghone ukukhuluma , ufunde bewutlole , isiNgisi njengelinye lamalimi wangokomthetho .
uvume ukuthathwa igadangiso lemino begodu kufanele kube akhenge ufunyanwe unomlandu wobulelesi namkha kube usazokutjhutjhiswa .
uzimisele ukubandulwa .
uzimisele ukwenza isifungo .
ungabi nemigwalo ebonakalako emzimbeni ( ama ) ; begodu .
kunyulwa bona ube nelayisense yokutjhayela , nanyana kungasi yifuneko emarizeveni . .
Khuyini inturhu yangekhaya ? .
Ngokuya komThetho weNturhu yangeKhaya : .
mhlobo omunye nomunye wokutlhorisa ofaka ukutlhorisa ngokommoya , umseme , ngokomzimba namkha ngakwezomnotho .
ukona ipahla .
ukulandelela .
ukungena endaweni yomuntu ngaphandle kwemvumo .
okhunye nokhunye ukutlhorisa namkha ukulawula lapho ukuziphatha okunjalo kubanga ukulimala namkha kungaba yingozi epilweni yakho , ukuphepha namkha ukuphila kuhle . .
Nayikuthi lemihlobo yokutlhorisa iyenzeka kuwe namkha komunye omaziko ungenza isibawo somlayo wokuvikelwa . .
Umlayo wokuvikelwa enturhwini yangekhaya mtlolo okhutjhwa yikhotho okhandela umtlhorisi : .
ekwenzeni isenzo senturhu yangekhaya .
ekufuneni irhelebho lomunye umuntu ekwenzeni isenzo esinjalo .
ukungena endaweni yokuhlala eyabelwana mnghonghoyili kanye noziphendulelako .
ukungena ehlangothini elithileko lendawo yokuhlala enjalo .
ukungena endaweni yokuhlala yomnghonghoyili .
ukungena endaweni yokusebenzela yomnghonghoyili .
ukukhandela umnghonghoyili ngokujayelekileko ohlala namkha obekabelana ngendawo yokuhlala ukungena namkha ukuhlala endaweni yokuhlala okwabelwana ngayo namkha ihlangothi elithileko layo .
ukwenza esinye nesinye isenzo esibekwe emlayweni wokuvikelwa . .
Ngubani ongenza isibawo somlayo wokuvikelwa ? .
Ngomunye nomunye otlhoriswako namkha owakhe watlhoriswa .
Mntwana , ongenza isibawo angarhelejwa .
Ngomunye nomunye umuntu onekareko epilweni yomnghonghoyili . .
Abantu abalandelako bangenza isibawo ngemvumo etloliweko yomnghonghoyili ngaphandle kwalokha umnghonghoyili nakamntwana , amumuntu ogula ngomkhumbulo , ayathile namkha nayikuthi ikhotho iyaneliswa bona akakghoni ukunikela ngemvumo etloliweko : .
omnikeli werhelebho lezengqondo .
isisebenzi sezamaphilo .
ipholisa .
isisebenzi sezehlalakuhle .
utitjhere .
Nawufuna ilwazi elinabileko , yiya ku yomNyango wezoBulungiswa nokuThuthukiswa komThethosisekelo . .
Amagadango okufanele alandelwe .
Yenza isibawo somlayo wokuvikelwa eKhotho kaMarhastrada eseduze nalapho uhlala khona namkha usebenza khona ngesinye nesinye isikhathi , ngesikhathi nangemva kwesikhathi sokusebenza kwekhotho begodu nangamalanga wokuphumula namkha iimpelaveke . .
Kokuthoma yenza isibawo somLayo wokuVikelwa wesiKhatjhana ( i Protection Order ) ngokuzalisa iForomo 6 : Interim Protection Order ( UmLayo wokuVikelwa wesiKhatjhana ) eKhotho kaMarhastrada namkha ePhakamileko eseduze . .
Nasele wenze isibawo somLayo wokuVikelwa wesiKhatjhana , zalisa iForomo 2 : Application for Protection Order ( Isibawo somLayo wokuVikelwa ) eKhotho kaMarhastrada namkha ePhakamileko eseduze . .
Isibawo kufanele senziwe ngencwadi yesifungo ebeka : .
Amaqiniso isibawo esisekelwe kiwo .
Ubunjalo bomlayo obawiwako .
Igama lesitetjhi samapholisa lapho umnghonghoyili angahle abike khona ukwephulwa komlayo wokuvikelwa ofunwako . .
Lapho isibawo silethwa ngokwenzela umnghonghoyili ngomunye umuntu , incwadi yesifungo kufanele ibeke : .
amabanga enza omunye umuntu abe nekareko ekuphileni kuhle komnghonghoyili .
umsebenzi womunye umuntu kanye nesikhundla enza ngaso isibawo .
imvumo etloliweko ebuya kumnghonghoyili , ngaphandle kwebujameni lapho umnghonghoyili : .
amntwana .
akhubazeke ngokwengqondo .
ayathile .
amumuntu ikhotho eyaneliswa bona akakghoni ukunikela ngemvumo efunekako . .
Qinisekisa iforomo nomabhalana wekhotho bewulilethe . .
Umabhalana uzakuthumela isibawo sakho kumarhastrada ozakubeka ilanga lokobana ubuye ekhotho khona isibawo sakho sizakutjhejwa . .
Umarhastrada godu uzakulungisa isaziso sokwazisa umtlhorisi ngomlayo wokuvikelwa nokobana eze nini ekhotho . .
Ngemva kokuvela ekhotho , umarhastrada anganikela ngomlayo wokuvikelwa . .
Kungebangalani kufanele uzitlolise ? .
ukwenza umsebenzi wesiphrofetjhinali .
ukusebenzisa igama langokomthetho nethayithili ethi sosayensi wemvelo namkha ukugadangisa isirhunyezo esibekiweko ngemva kwegama lakho ( isibonelo , Pr.Sci.Nat. ) .
ukusebenza ngokubonisana .
ukufumana ubujamo besiphrofetjhinali nokuzibandakanya emivuzweni enikelwa ziinkhungo zeemali .
ukuthabela ukusekelwa mkhandlu nesiqinisekiso esingathathi hlangothi mayelana nekghono lakho .
ukuvikela nokuqinisa umsebenzi wesiphrofetjhinali . .
Khuyini iimfuneko zokuzitlolisa ? .
nasiya ekuzitloliseni njengososayensi wemvelo wesiphrofetjhinali - idigri namkha idiploma yeminyaka emi kanye nelemuko leminyaka emithathu .
nasiya ekuzitloliseni njengososayensi wemvelo ofuna umsebenzi - idigri namkha idiploma yeminyaka emi ngaphandle kwelemuko .
nasiya ekuzitloliseni njengososayensi wemvelo oqinisekisiweko - idigri namkha idiploma yeminyaka emi nelemuko lomnyaka munye . .
Amahlangothi wokuzitlolisa angendlela elandelako : .
USosayensi wemVelo wesiPhrofetjhinali ( Pr.Sci.Nat. ) .
USosayensi wemVelo oFuna umSebenzi ( Cand.Sci.Nat. ) .
USosayensi wemVelo oQinisekisiweko ( Cert.Sci.Nat. ) .

Zinikela ngokuqaleka okuhlukileko emakethe / lapho zithengiswa khona , begodu zingasebenza emkhiqizweni namkha emsebenzini eziwenzako . .

Zalisa izinga ku weforomo i . .

Kumele utjheje bonyana ungafaki ipahla namkha imisebenzi esemazingeni ahlukileko esibaweni esisodwa setshwayo lerhwebo . .
Nawenze njalo ' ufanele ukulungisa ihlathululo ukuze ifake ipahla namkha umsebenzi okhambelana nezinga elilodwa elithileko . .
Okhunye okuseleko , ufanele wenze isibawo esinye ngobutjha . .
Iziko 74 leforomo I " I yomsebenzi " kulapho uzakuthola khona imitlolo yokuthintana evela e letshwayo lebhizinisi . .
Nangabe i le iyatjhuguluka , kumele wazise umNyango ngokufaneleko ngokubawa irhelebho lokutjhugulula i eforomeni i . .
Isibawo sakho nasikhambelana nazo zoke iimfuneko ezibekiweko , uzakunikelwa ilanga nenomboro yesibawo . .
Ukuthintana okuzakwenzeka kuzabe kusetjenziswa inomboro yesibawo leso . .
Nanyana kuthatha isikhathi esingange ukutlolisa itshwayo lebhizinisi nawuthoma ukulisebenzisa emva kokufumana inomboro yesibawo . .
Nangabe itshwayo lakho lamukelwe ngaphandle kwenthikamezo , kumele ulikhangise eNcwadini yamaPhathenti , egadangiswa njalo ngenyanga baGadangisi bakaRhulumende . .

Nangabe kunokuphikisa okutholakalako , umTlolisi wamaTshwayo weBhizinisi webo uzakubiza umhlangano hlangana nomphikisako kanye nombawi . .

Nawubhadala ebhankeni sebenzisa ikhowudu yekhastama . .
Umuntu otjhonileko mumuntu okolodako ilifa lakhe ( yoke into , kufaka imali umuntu ayikolodako ) elithethwe ngokomthetho ( libekwe ngaphasi kwelawulo ukufika lapho azakukghona ukubhadela isikolodo ) . .
Nayikuthi utjhade ngokuhlanganyela ipahla begodu othethene naye uyatjhona , umThetho wokuTjhona ka nawe ukuthatha njengotjhonileko . .
Nayikuthi otjhonileko ufuna ukuthathwa njengongakatjhoni eminyakeni elitjhumi yokuthathwa njengotjhonileko , angenza isibawo sokubuyiselwa ebujameni bangaphambilini . .
Ngubani ongenza isibawo sokubuyiselwa ebujameni bangaphambilini ? .
ngotjhonileko .
yi egunyaziweko yotjhonileko , nayikuthi otjhonileko akahlali eSewula Afrika .
mhlolokazi namkha umfelwa wotjhonileko , nayikuthi bebatjhade ngokuhlanganyela ipahla .
obekathethwe ngotjhonileko ngaphambilini , nayikuthi bebatjhade ngokuhlanganyela ipahla .
ngophetha iimfiso zewili ( i ) yelifa lohlongakeleko otjhonileko . .
Otjhonileko angenza isibawo sokubuyiselwa ebujameni bangaphambilini msinyana kangangani ngemva kokuthathelwa ilifa ngokomthetho ? .
Kwesinye nesinye isikhathi : .
msinyana ngemva kobana zoke iinkolodo ezokolodwako zibhadelwe kanye neendleko zokuthathwa ngokomthetho kwelifa zibhadelwe ngokuzeleko .
nayikuthi otjhonileko wenza isibopho sangokomthetho sokubhadela isikolodo esamukelwa ngabathintekako namkha abakolodako ngokwesibalo nenani , begodu otjhonileko ubhadele namkha unikele ngesiqinisekiso . .
Ngemva kwenyanga ezisithandathu : .
nayikuthi kungakapheli iinyanga ezisithandathu lezi , akunasikolodo esifunwe elifeni lotjhonileko begodu ngokuya kobujamo bokobana : .
lokhu kukokuthoma ukobana otjhonileko athathelwe ilifa ngokomthetho .
otjhonileko akakafunyanwa anomlandu wokwephulwa komthetho okuthileko . .
Ngemva kweenyanga ezilitjhumi nambili ukuthoma ngelanga lesiqinisekiso saka se yokuthoma ye elifeni begodu ngokuya kobujamo bokobana : .
lokhu kukokuthoma ukobana otjhonileko athathelwe ilifa ngokomthetho .
otjhonileko akakafunyanwa anomlandu wokwephulwa komthetho okuthileko . .
Ngemva kweminyaka emithathu : .
ukuthoma ngelanga lesiqinisekiso saka e yokuthoma ye elifeni nayikuthi otjhonileko besekhe wathathelwa ilifa ngokomthetho ukudlula ihlandla linye kodwana bekangakafunyanwa anomlandu wokwephulwa komthetho okuthileko . .
Ngemva kweminyaka emihlanu : .
ebujameni botjhonileko ongakafunyanwa anomlandu wokwephula umthetho . .
Ngemva kweminyaka elitjhumi : .
otjhonileko kufanele athathwe njengobuyiselwe ebujameni bangaphambilini - ngaphandle kwalokha , kungakapheli iminyaka elitjhumi yokobana ikhotho ithethe omunye njengotjhonileko , umuntu onekareko wenza isibawo ekhotho bona ingabuyiseli ebujameni bangaphambilini otjhonileko begodu isibawo leso siyavunywa . .
Amagadango okufanele alandelwe .
Angeze wenza isibawo sokubuyiselwa ebujameni bangaphambilini ngokwakho kodwana uzakutlhoga irhelebho lezomthetho . .
Ilifa lomuntu ohlongakeleko liba khona lokha umuntu nakahlongakalako begodu atjhiya ipahla kanye / namkha umtlolo oyiwili namkha othathwa njengewili . .
Ilifa kufanele liphathwe belisatjalaliswe ngokuya kwewili yohlongakeleko namkha nayikuthi ohlongakeleko akakatjhiyi iwili , ngokuya kweenjamiso zomthetho . .
UmThetho wokuPhathwa kwamaFa ka , ubeka ikambiso ezakulandelwa ukuphatha ilifa lohlongakeleko . .
Ilifa lohlongakeleko kufanele libikwe ku kungakapheli amalanga ali welanga lokuhlongakala . .
Ukuhlongakala kungabikwa ngomunye nomunye umuntu olawula namkha ophethe umtlolo womuntu ohlongakeleko oyiwili namkha othathwa njengewili . .
Kufanele kubikwe nini ukuhlongakala ku ? .
Nayikuthi umuntu ohlongakeleko uhlongakalele eSewula Afrika begodu utjhiye ipahla kanye / namkha omunye nomunye umtlolo oyiwili namkha othathwa njengewili .
Nayikuthi ohlongakeleko wahlongakalela ngaphandle kweSewula Afrika , kodwana watjhiya ipahla eSewula Afrika kanye / namkha nomtlolo oyiwili namkha othathwa njengewili . .
Libikwa kuphi ilifa lomuntu ohlongakeleko ? .
Nanyana woke ama kamarhastrada aziindawo zokusebenzela zaka lapho amafa wabahlongakeleko abikwa khona , anamandla wangokomthetho aqintelweko begodu azakudlulisela woke amafa anamawili kanye namafa adlula i 000 ngenani e lephrovinsi laka . .
Nawufisa ukubika ilifa elinjalo , kuhle wenze njalo bunqopha e laka . .
Nayikuthi inani lelifa lingaphasi kwe 000 , bika ilifa e lakamarhastrada . .
Nayikuthi lidlula i 000 , bika bunqopha e laka . .

nayikuthi ohlongakeleko bekangahlali eSewula Afrika ngesikhathi sokuhlongakala , bika ilifa komunye nomunye ( kodwana kungapheleli koyedwa ) u .

ungafumana iforomo lesaziso sokuhlongakala neminye imitlolo yokubika kwelinye nelinye i laka wekhotho ephakamileko namkha kwelinye nelinye i lakamarhastrada .
inani lelifa kanye nomhlobo wesikhundla esifunekako uzakuqunta ngemitlolo ozayizalisa bewuyilethe . .

isitifikeyidi samambala sokuhlongakala namkha ikhophi eqinisekisiweko yaso .
isitifikeyidi samambala somtjhado namkha ikhophi eqinisekisiweko yaso - nayifunekako .

irhemo labanikeli beenkolodo bohlongakeleko - nalifunekako .
isifungo esiqinisekisa bona ilifa sele libikiwe komunye u namkha kwenye indawo yokusebenzela ka . .
Nayikuthi ilifa lingaphasi kwe 000 , u angasebenza ngaphandle kwencwadi yokuphethwa kweemfiso zewili esikhundleni salokho akhuphe iincwadi zesigunyazo ngokuya kwesiGaba 18(3) somThetho wokuPhathwa kwamaFa ka . .
Nayikuthi inani lelifa lidlula i 000 , zalisa imitlolo elandelako : .
isaziso sokuhlongakala .
incwadi yesifungo : Imininingwana yesihlobo - elizakuzaliswa nayikuthi ohlongakeleko akhenge atjhiye iwili esebenzako ( Form J192 : Affidavit : particulars of next of kin ) . .
Isifungwesi , esenziwa sihlobo somuntu onzima ohlongakeleko , obekanganawili , kufanele sibeke bona ilifa alikabikwa ku namkha endaweni yokusebenzela ( nayikhona ) .
iforomo lerhemo .
ukuKhethwa njengozakuPhetha iimFuno zeWili / Iforomo lokukhethwa - elizakuzaliswa ziindlalifa ukukhomba umjameli ka : .
nayikuthi lilifa elinganawili namkha .
nayikuthi iwili ayikhombi othileko njengomphethi namkha .
nayikuthi okhonjwe njengomphethi uhlongakele namkha wale ukukhonjwa . .
